	<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">List of 2012 Indian Premier League personnel changes</h1>
	
	<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
		<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
		<div id="contentSub"></div>

		<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><p>
This is a list of all <b>personnel changes</b> for the <b><a href="/wiki/2012_Indian_Premier_League" title="2012 Indian Premier League">2012 Indian Premier League</a></b>.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Replacement_signings">Replacement signings</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_2012_Indian_Premier_League_personnel_changes&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Replacement signings">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Players were signed as replacement of contracted players who were not available to play due to injuries and national commitments. Under IPL rules, the replacements have to be chosen from the pool of players who went unsold in the auction, and cannot be paid more than the players they are replacing, though they can be paid less.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Auction">Auction</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_2012_Indian_Premier_League_personnel_changes&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Auction">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>
The players auction for the <a href="/wiki/2012_Indian_Premier_League" title="2012 Indian Premier League">2012 Indian Premier League</a> (fifth season) was held on 4 February 2012 in Bangalore.<sup id="cite_ref-auction_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auction-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> Each player in the auction pool had a base price under which franchise owners cannot bid. Players were allowed to set their base price between $20,000 to $400,000. The auction was telecast live on <a href="/wiki/SET_Max" class="mw-redirect" title="SET Max">SET Max</a>, the official broadcaster of IPL.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>IPL authority increased the number of players in each squad to 33 from the previous limit of 30 and also increased the salary cap by $2 million.<sup id="cite_ref-auction_20-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auction-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> Each team can have a maximum of 11 overseas players in their squad and they can spend up to $2 million at auction.
</p><p>The players of <a href="/wiki/Kochi_Tuskers_Kerala" title="Kochi Tuskers Kerala">Kochi Tuskers Kerala</a> were included in the players auction.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> Kochi was terminated by the <a href="/wiki/Board_of_Cricket_Control_in_India" class="mw-redirect" title="Board of Cricket Control in India">BCCI</a> in September 2011.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sold_players">Sold players</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_2012_Indian_Premier_League_personnel_changes&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Sold players">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

</p>

<ul><li><b>First tier ($ 400,000):</b></li></ul>
